It's on the shallow end of complexity. \r\n\r\nThe objective of the game is to get rid of your cards fast to win this game! \r\n\r\nBut Uno Classic game not just a feast of fun – it also helps develop kids counting, matching, critical thinking, and social interaction.\r\n\r\nUno is a simple color and number matching game. The deck consists of 108 cards, of which there are 25 of each color (red, green, blue, and yellow), each color having two of each rank except zero. The ranks in each color are zero to nine, \"Skip\", \"Draw Two\", and \"Reverse\" (the last three being \"action cards\"). In addition, the deck contains four each of \"Wild\" and \"Wild Draw Four\" cards\r\n\r\nEach player is dealt 7 cards and the remaining cards are placed face down to form a draw pile. \r\nThe first player has to match the card in the discard pile either by number or color or the player can throw down a Wild Card else he must pick a card from the draw pile. If he can play what is drawn, great. Otherwise play moves to the next person.\r\n\r\nIn Uno The card deck contains four colors with numbers from 0 to 9, as well as Action cards - \"Reverse\", \"Skip\", \"Take Two\", \"Wild\" and \"Wild Take Four\".\r\n\r\nThe winner is first one who has no cards left. \r\n\r\nNow you can play Uno Classic with your Facebook friends, against the computer or with millions of Uno players around the world.\r\n\r\nYou can also create a Private Room and invite your friends to play.\r\n\r\nThe biggest advantage of Uno Classic card game is that it can be enjoyed by everybody in the family.
